Accessibility digest

PageMeridian Senior Living

Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score1860
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1860, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 928. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 200. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 16. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue duplicateID

WCAG: 4.1.1

Score: 206

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package ibm, test RPT_Elem_UniqueId, score 204 (Element id attribute value is not unique within the document)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 72

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 70 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 51

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 49 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 43

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 30 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 8 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)
  • Package ibm, test IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA, score 20 (Contrast ratio of text with background does not meet WCAG 2.1 AA)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 39

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 37 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue leadingClipsText

WCAG: 1.4.8

Score: 38

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 144, score 36 (Line height is insufficent to properly display the computed font size)

Issue focusableOperable

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 31

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focOp, score 29 (Operable elements that cannot be Tab-focused and vice versa)

Issue figureNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 30

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package ibm, test HAAC_Figure_label, score 28 (figure element has no associated label)

Issue visibleLabelNotName

WCAG: 2.5.3

Score: 23

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test label-content-name-mismatch, score 11 (Element visible text is not part of its accessible name)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.2_5_3.F96, score 4 (Visible label is not in the accessible name)
  • Package ibm, test WCAG21_Label_Accessible, score 15 (Accessible name does not match or contain the visible label text)

Issue linkForcesNewWindow

WCAG: 3.2.5

Score: 23

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 218, score 21 (Link opens in a new window without user control)

Score: 15

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test motion, score 13 (Change of visible content not requested by user)

Issue titleBad

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 14

Issue reports in this category:

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 14

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 95, score 3 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))

Issue headingStructure

Score: 9

  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_3_1_AAA.G141, score 6 (Heading level is incorrect)
  • Package tenon, test 155, score 1 (Headings are not structured in a hierarchical manner)

Issue contrastRisk

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 9

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_3_F24.F24.FGColour, score 1 (Inline foreground color may lack a complementary background color)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Abs, score 5 (Contrast between the absolutely positioned text and its background may be less than 7:1)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Abs, score 1 (Contrast between the absolutely positioned text and its background may be less than 4.5:1)
